################
# NAME FORMATS #
################

### Imperial Militarist 

# Imperial Militarist 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 4
			OR = {
				has_government = "gov_star_empire"
				has_government = "gov_martial_empire"
			}
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
			# home_planet = { always = yes }
		}
	}
	format = "format.ben_imp_mil.1"
	prefix_format = "[This.Capital.System.GetName] <imperial_mil>"
	noun = "[This.Capital.System.GetName]"
	# Empire of Sol
}

# Imperial Militarist 2
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			OR = {
				has_government = "gov_star_empire"
				has_government = "gov_martial_empire"
			}
			is_pirate = no

			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
			# home_planet = { always = yes }
		}
	}
	format = "format.ben_imp_mil.2"
	prefix_format = "[This.Capital.System.GetName] <imperial_mil>"
	noun = "[This.Capital.System.GetName]"
	# Great Empire of Sol
}

# Democratic Generic 9

	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 8
			has_government = gov_representative_democracy
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
			NOT = { has_civic = civic_socialistic }

	# Earth Empire

# Religion 1
empire_name_format = {
	random_weight = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 8
			OR = {
				has_government = "gov_theocratic_republic"
				has_government = "gov_theocratic_oligarchy"
				has_government = "gov_holy_tribunal"
				has_government = "gov_theocratic_dictatorship"
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
				has_ethic = ethic_militarist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_pacifist }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_xenophile }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_militarist }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe }
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_green }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_green }
			NOT = { has_civic = civic_environmentalist }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_industrial }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_industrial }
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			has_country_flag = radical_cult
		}
	}
	format = "format.ben_rel_gen.1"
	prefix_format = "<rel_adj>"
	noun = "[This.Capital.GetName]"
	# True Church
}

			add = 4

				has_government = gov_constitutional_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_representative_democracy
				has_government = gov_military_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_military_junta
				has_government = gov_military_commissariat
				has_government = gov_totalitarian_regime
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_technocratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_enlightened_dictatorship
			}
			has_civic = civic_socialistic
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no

			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
			# home_planet = { always = yes }
		}
	}

				has_government = gov_totalitarian_regime
				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_technocratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_enlightened_dictatorship
			}
			has_civic = civic_socialistic
			is_pirate = no
			is_primitive = no
			NOT = { is_country_type = fallen_empire }
			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
			# home_planet = { always = yes }
		}
	}
	format = "format.socialist.2"
	prefix_format = "<socialist_desc> [This.Capital.GetName] <socialist>"
	noun = "[This.Capital.GetName]"
	# Great Empire of Earth
}

		modifier = {
			add = 16

				has_government = gov_constitutional_dictatorship

				has_government = gov_military_dictatorship

				has_government = gov_executive_committee
				has_government = gov_technocratic_dictatorship
				has_government = gov_enlightened_dictatorship
			}

				has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe

			NOT = { is_country_type = awakened_fallen_empire }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = radical_cult }
		}
	}
